ZER BA AE YIN GSUNGS PA LA, NGAS DENG SANG YUL DUS

'DIR GRAGS TSOD KYI THA SNYAD LA LTOS TE RI BONG RVA MED ZER BA
YIN, YUL DUS THAMS CAD DU MED ZER BA MIN MOD, RI BONG LA RVA YOD
PA'I GTAM RGYUD KYANG SNANG ZHUS PAS, 'O DE GA RANG YIN

YOD MED THAMS CAD YUL DUS DE'I THA SNYAD TZAM ZHIG LA LTOS TE
'JOG DGOS, YUL 'GA' ZHIG NA DNGUL RDO TSAD KYI MING LA DNGUL GYI
GZUGS BRNYAN ZER, RANG RES DNGUL GYI GZUGS BRNYAN

@064A *, ,ZER BA 'DI LA DEN DNGUL RDO TSAD ZER, DE'I PHYIR DEN
DNGUL RDO TSAD KYIS PHAN GNOD CHUNG, DNGUL GYI GZUGS BRNYAN GYIS
PHAN GNOD CHEN PO BYED PA YIN GSUNG GSUNGS,

YANG 'JIG RTEN RANG GA BA'I BLO LHAN SKYES LA TSOGS RGYUN GCIG
DANG DU MA'I 'CHAR LUGS KYI DPER, RVA STOD RDO RJE 'CHANG GIS,
MI ZHIG GI LHAM SNGA LO CHUS KHYER BA'I CHU KHA DER PHYI LO
BSLEBS PA NA,

NGA'I LHAM CHU 'DIS KHYER ZHES SNGA PHYI GCIG TU 'CHAR BA LTA BU
DANG, RI MGON NAGS YOD PA MES TSIG PA'I PHYI LO NA NING DE NA
NAGS YOD DA LO MI 'DUG ,CES NA NING GI RI DANG DA LO'I RI SO SOR
PHYE

NAS BZUNG BA LTA BU RED GSUNGS, CHOS GANG LA YANG MTHA' GCIG TU
BDEN PAR GRUB PA MED PAS, NGA TSOS NYIN LAM MANG PO YIN PA BYA
RGOD DANG RDZU 'PHRUL CAN SOGS KYIS, NYIN LAM GCIG

DANG YUD TZAM ZHIG GI LAM YIN PAR 'GYUR BA DANG, GANG ZAG GCIG
LA'ANG MI SKYA DANG RAB BYUNG GI DUS MING SO SOR BTAGS PAS, DE
DANG DE YIN PAR 'GYUR PA SOGS LA BLTAS NA THA SNYAD SHIN TU

DBANG CHE BA RED, DE'I MTSON NAS CHOS THAMS CAD RANG NGOS NAS MA
GRUB PA MING DU BTAGS PA TZAM YIN, DE GA RANG GIS TSIM DGOS
GSUNGS, AA KA BRTZON 'GRUS ZER BA'I DGE BSHES

CHEN PO DE LA GRVA BA GCIG GIS, KUN RIG 'DI THEG CHEN GYI CHOS
AE YIN ZHUS PAR, 'O KUN RIG 'DI THEG CHEN PAS BTON NA THEG CHEN
GYI CHOS RED, THEG DMAN PAS BTON NA THEG DMAN GYI

@064B CHOS RED, NGED RANG GNYIS 'DRA MOS BTON NA GANG YANG MA
RED GSUNGS 'DUG ,YANG AA KA 'DI BAS PHYI DRO GLING SKOR DU PHEBS
SKABS KHYI LA SBYIN PA GTONG RGYU'I RTZAM PA BRDZI BA NA PHYAG
DANG BZHES

PHOR BKRUS, DE NAS ZAN BRDZI BA LA GRVA BA ZHIG GIS DE 'DRA'I
GTZANG SBRA MDZAD CI DGOS ZHUS PAS, RANG RE'I SNANG TSOD LA NGES
PA CI YOD KHYI LA SBYIN PA BTANG NAS TSOGS GSOG PA LAS

BYANG CHUB SEMS DPA' 'DRA SBAGS NAS MNOL DU 'JUG NYEN YOD GSUNGS
PA RED GSUNGS, GO LNGA PA'I NYIN PHRENG DU 'JUG PA LAS, DE KHO
NA NYID GTAN LA 'BEBS PA'I RIGS PA GSUM

GSUNGS PA RNAMS ZER DGOS PA RED GSUNGS, GO BDUN PA DANG GO
BRGYAD PA'I NGOS SU THA SNYAD DU YOD PA LA 'JIG RTEN GYI GRAGS
PAS MI GNOD PA DANG GCIG ,THA SNYAD PA'I TSAD MA

GZHAN GYIS MI GNOD PA DANG GNYIS, DON DAM DPYOD PA'I RIG SHES
KYIS MI GNOD PA DANG GSUM TSANG DGOS PAR BSTAN GSUNGS, STON PA'I
SKU 'DI SGROL MA'I SKU YIN PA LA THA SNYAD PA'I

TSAD MAS GNOD, DE LA 'JIG RTEN DANG BSTAN BCOS LA GRAGS PAS
KYANG GNOD, DE LTAR BDEN PAR GRUB PA LA RIG SHES KYIS GNOD, STON
PA'I SKU THA SNYAD TZAM DU YOD PA LA DE DAG GANG

GIS KYANG MI GNOD, GO BRGYAD PA'I RGYAB PHRENG DU GO RGYU CHEN
PO GSUNG 'DUG GSUNGS, GO DGU PA'I RGYAB PHRENG DU 'OD SRUNGS
KYIS ZHUS PAR, GANG STONG PA NYID KYIS CHOS RNAMS STONG PAR MI
BYED

@065A *, ,GSUNGS PA'I DON NI, STONG NYID RANG LA LTOS TE STONG
NYID MIN, DGAG BYA LA LTOS TE STONG NYID YIN GSUNGS PA RED
GSUNGS, DE'I NYIN PHRENG GSUM PA DANG BZHI BAR DPYAD

RGYU CHE ZHING, GNAD BSDUS NA CHOS RNAMS RANG GI MTSAN NYID KYIS
GRUB PAS STONG PA NI, RANG GI NGO BOS STONG PA'I DON DANG, DE
LAS GZHAN PA'I STONG TSUL RNAMS DE MIN PA'I RGYU MTSAN NI, BYE

MDO DANG RNAM RIG PAS BSHAD PA'I STONG TSUL GYI DON TSAD MAS
GRUB ZIN BYED PA MA NYAMS KYANG, YID DANG NGAG GI GRUB MTHA' 'AM
DAM BCAS BDEN GRUB TU DNGOS SU SGRO 'DOGS PA YOD LA, RANG

RGYUD PAS BSHAD PA'I STONG TSUL GYI DON TSAD MAS GRUB ZIN BYED
PA MA NYAMS KYANG, GRUB MTHA' 'AM DAM BCAS DNGOS SU BDEN GRUB
YIN MI ZER RUNG, BDEN GRUB KYI DON KHAS BLANGS PA'I SGO

NAS SGRO 'DOGS PAR BYED PA MI 'GAL ZHING, RANG GI MTSAN NYID
KYIS GRUB PA'I STONG TSUL DE TSAD MAS GRUB ZIN BYED PA MA NYAMS
PA'I RANG LA GRUB MTHAS BLO BSGYUR BA'I SGO NAS, GZHI GANG

YANG BDEN PAR GRUB PA'AM BDEN PAR GRUB PA'I DON DU SGRO 'DOGS
PA'I SGRO 'DOGS KUN BTAGS SKYE MI SRID GSUNGS, ,CES DRANG BA
DANG NGES PA'I DON RNAM PAR 'BYED PA'I BSTAN BCOS LEGS PAR

BSHAD PA'I SNYING PO'I ZIN BRIS DKA' GNAS GSAL BAR BYED PA'I
SGRON ME ZHES BYA 'DI NI, BLA MA RDO RJE 'CHANG CHEN PO SHING BZA'
PAntI TA'I ZHAL SNGA NAS KYIS, LEGS BSHAD SNYING PO'I BSHAD LUNG
RGYAS PAR GNANG SKABS,

@065B MKHAS PA 'GA' ZHIG GIS ZIN BRIS MDZAD PA LA DPE RGYUN SHIN
TU DKON ZHING, AA RIG MKHAN RIN PO CHE'I PHYAG DPE'I KHROD DU
SHOG DRIL THA BCU GSUM TZAM 'DUG PA GCIG DANG, GLU RTZE DGE
BSHES RIN PO CHE'I PHYAG DPE'I KHOD

DU'ANG DE LA MA DPE BYAS PA AE YIN SNYAM PA ZHIG STE, MJUG CUNG
ZAD MA TSANG BA GNYIS 'DUG PA TSIG SNA BSDU LUGS DANG, TSIG ZUR
CUNG ZAD RE MA GTOGS PHAL CHER GCIG PAR 'DUG LA, MJUG MA TSANG
BA'ANG SHOG DRIL

'KHYAR BA 'AM SAM tA'I NGOS NAS LUS PA GANG RUNG DU SNANG, SHOG
DRIL DE LAS GCIG SHOS LA YI GE MANG DU CHAD PA DANG, SKABS 'GA'
ZHIG TU THIG SHAR RE GNYIS TZAM CHAD PA'ANG 'DUG PA DANG, YANG
DE GNYIS LA

SKABS SKABS NA GSUNG BSHAD 'GA' ZHIG GZHUNG DANG BSTUN NAS 'BRI
DUS GONG 'OG 'KHRUGS PAR MNGON PA SOGS ZHU DAG CUNG ZAD DGOS PA
RNAMS BYAS, YI GE 'BA' ZHIG DPYAD GZHIR SNANG YANG THAG GCOD
DKA' BA

RNAMS RANG SOR BZHAG NAS DPE RGYUN 'DI NYID MI NYAMS PA'I PHYIR
DU BRIS PA 'DI YANG RJE BTZUN BLA MA'I THUGS KYI DGONGS PA YONGS
SU RDZOGS TE, TSE RABS THAMS CAD DU GSUNG GI GSANG BA 'DZIN PA'I
SRAS KYI THU BOR 'GYUR PA'I RGYUR

GYUR CIG, *, ,NA MO GU RU BHYEE: RGYAL GSUNG BRGYAD KHRI BZHI
STONG SNYING PO MCHOG ,SHER PHYIN MDO YI DNGOS BSTAN ZAB MO'I
DON, ,JI BZHIN GZIGS PA KLU SGRUB THOGS MED CES, ,SA GSUM SNYAN
PAR

GRAGS PA ZUNG LA 'DUD, ,DE GNYIS DGONGS PA JI BZHIN DBU SEMS
KYI, ,LTA BA'I GNAD KUN GSAL BAR STON PA'I GZHUNG, ,DRANG DES
RNAM PAR 'BYED PA'I LEGS BSHAD CHE, ,'JAM DPAL SNYING PO

@066A *, ,ZHES BYA'I ZHAL LAS BYUNG, ,GANG GI GSUNG RAB DGONGS
ZAB 'O MA'I MTSO, ,BLO GROS BZANG PO'I SRUB SHING GIS BSRUBS PAS,
LEGS BSHAD MAR GYI NYING KHU 'DI THON PAS, ,

BSHAD SGRUB DAR ZHING RGYAS PA'I GSOS SU GYUR, ,GZHUNG 'DIR THOS
BSAM SGEM PAS 'JUG RNAMS LA, ,PHAN PHYIR PAR GYI CHOS SBYIN SPEL
BA 'DI, ,MKHAS BTZUN BZANG POS GRAGS PAS DBUS GTZANG KUN, ,

KHYAB PA'I BSHES GNYEN KAL WA'I MTSAN CAN GYI, ,YANG SPRUL BLO
BZANG BKRA SHIS KYIS MTSON PA'I, ,RGYU SBYOR YIG 'DRI NGAG DBANG
BZANG PO DANG, ,BRKOS MKHAN BLO BZANG CHOS 'PHEL 'BREL THOGS KUN,
,SKYE DANG SKYE

BAR 'JAM MGON BSTAN DANG MJAL, ,YANG DAG LTA BA RTOGS PA'I MTSON
RNON GYIS, ,BDAG TU 'DZIN PA'I DRA BA RAB BCAD DE, ,THAR BA'I
KHANG BZANG MCHOG DER BGROD PAR SHOG ,BSTAN PA'I DPAL GYUR MGON
RNAMS ZHABS

PAD BRTAN, ,DGE 'DUN SDE RNAMS MTHUN ZHING THOS BSAM BRTZON,
,BSTAN PA'I SBYIN BDAG TSOGS RNAMS STOBS 'BYOR 'PHEL, ,KUN KYANG
PHAN TSUN DGA' BDES 'TSO BAR SHOG ,DGA' LDAN LUGS BZANG GSER

MDOG 'CHANG BA'I SDE, ,BKRA SHIS KUN 'BYUNG NOR BU BSAM 'PHEL
GLING, ,JI SRID LHUN PO GNAS PA DE SRID DU, ,NAM YANG MI NUB DAR
ZHING RGYAS GYUR CIG ,CES DRANG NGES RNAM 'BYED GYI ZIN BRIS
'DI'I DPE RGYUN DKON STABS

SPRUL SKU BLO BZANG BKRA SHIS PAS SBYIN BDAG BYAS TE, CHOS
SBYIN RGYA CHER SPEL PHYIR BRTZI BZHAG SLOB DPON DAM PA DGE 'DUN
RGYA MTSO NAS PAR GSAR BSKRUN MDZAD SKABS, PAR BYANG SMON
TSIG 'DI NI, SH'AKYA'I DGE SBYONG NGAG DBANG DAR RGYAS GYIS
SMRAS PA'O,,
